# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
Point where the function change from increasing to decreasing or vice versa, the derivative
goes from negative to positive or from positive to negative. In general, points where the 
derivative goes to 0, if goes from negative to positive it is a local min, if positive to negative
a local max and if only touches the 0 it is a horizontal point of inflection ^0vfLD2Ki

%%
